[30;1m153 | [0m[35m~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[0m
[30;1m154 | [0m[35mAny hash function in the :code:`hashlib` module (:code:`md5, sha1, sha224, sha256, sha384, sha512`)[0m
[30;1m155 | [0m[35mwill work, as will any hash function that implements the same interface / core functionality as the[0m
[30;1m156 | [0m[35mthose in :code:`hashlib`. For instance, if you wish to use SHA3 as the hash function the[0m
[30;1m157 | [0m[35m:code:`pysha3` package will work with this library as long as it is at version >=1.0b1 (as previous[0m
[30;1m158 | [0m[35mversions didn't work with the :code:`hmac` module which is used in nonce generation). Note[0m
[30;1m159 | [0m[35mthat :code:`sha3_224, sha3_256, sha3_384, sha3_512` are all in :code:`hashlib` as of python3.6.[0m
